Actually there's usually an emergency release latch inside car trunks (it looks like a tag), so try that. Also not to put a bummer on things, but generally speaking your odds of survival in a real-life abduction drop significantly if you are taken to a second location.   Generally speaking if someone is trying to force you to go to a secondary, then you are at a 90% chance of not making it out alive. There are hundreds of real murders where people, mainly women, are abducted at the threat of violence and are later found murdered and oftentimes raped. Even in cases of people being kidnapped and held hostage like this, they rarely make it out alive. The real advice here that anyone will give you is this; do NOT let an abductor take you to a secondary location, you're going to want to make a lot of noise like screaming or set off an alarm. Even if someone is pointing a gun at you, you need to run and get away. Do not comply, RUN. Even if you get shot at, your odds of survival are better at a primary location than they are at a secondary.

For the most flavorful and tender results, salt your steaks at least 40 minutes before or even the night before you plan to cook them. This takes a little planning, but â€œdry briningâ€ your steaks, will not only season the beef, but help them to retain moisture for a juicy, tender bite. Dry the steaks and leave the fat on. Set up your grill to have one hot zone and one cool zone. This can be done by turning on half of your burners or putting the coals just on one side of your grill. The side without burners or coals underneath it is where the steaks will begin. This lower, indirect heat will help raise the internal temperature so when you transfer it to the hot side of the grill you can sear it quickly and not end up with charred meat that is still raw inside. The timing. As a rule of thumb (for a steak 22mm thick) â€“ cook 2 minutes each side for rare, 3-4 mins each side for medium-rare and 4-6 mins each side for medium. For well done, cook for 2-4 minutes each side, then turn the heat down and cook for another 4-6 minutes. To test for doneness, use the tip of your clean index finger (or tongs) to gently prod the steak. Any firmer than that and itâ€™s on its way to well done. Allow the steaks to rest. Place the steaks onto a wooden board or plate, cover loosely with foil and rest for about 6-7 minutes before slicing across the grain or serving. I think the girl who bought them a television had Stockholm syndrome.    So that really took a dark turn.  I think a few of the hacks could work if they were executed better.  For instance, on certain kinds of matches will ignite when scratched against a hard surface.  Most matches are safety matches that must be struck against the match book.  And it's very unlikely you would get matches thrown at you.  But it is possible that you would be making your escape with your hands still tied and find some kind of flame along the way.  A stove, some matches, or a cigarette lighter.  And zip ties would be a pretty common way for a kidnapper to secure your hands.  So that part is pretty plausible.  As for inhaling while being tied up.  Maybe not the most effective thing to do.  But there might be other ways to make yourself a little larger while being tied up.  Maybe have your hands a little further from your body, etc.  You just need to be careful that the kidnapper doesn't notice what you are doing.  And that might make it a little easier to slip out of your ropes.  But, generally speaking, following life hacks when you are kidnapped might not be the best idea.

A VERY interesting fact about breathing in while being tied up was actually how Houdini (and later used by performer magician Chris Angel) escaped all those traps where they were tied up and bound, then placed in dangerous situations. It is a classic old magician's tactic used in actual performances when they are really tied up and placed in danger. FYI the CORRECT method to do this is to breathe in and tense your muscles ONLY when they are tensing the bindings.

Regarding melting a zip tie with a match: I'm pretty sure Troom Troom took this from the real life case in which one of serial killer Bob Berdella's victims escaped using this method. However, the reason he was able to do this was because Bob Berdella had been sexually assaulting him for a long period of time and was deluded into believing that his victim was actually in love with him, so he became more lax in his restraints when he left for work. The reason the victim couldn't simply bend at the waist to pick up the match was because he was tied to a bed post. Naturally, Troom Troom wasn't going to include any of these disturbing details and wanted to present a sanitised version of kidnapping in which the victim is never in too much danger, so the context is lost and this tip seems really bizarre as a result. I imagine the rest of these tips are similar: Things that have been/could be legit avenues of escape in specific circumstances, but without those circumstances it just seems weird and useless.

Snapping someones neck in the way she is doing it will very likely kill someone. The issue is the location on the spine. Generally, snapping a specific area of the spine results in, from lowest part of spine to the top, 1) no paralysis (lower parts such as directly above the coccyx), 2) leg-down paralysis 3) neck-down paralysis, 4) full paralysis or 5) death. Death mostly occurs when you break the top-most vertebrae, such as if a massive brown bear were to step on your neck. The vertebrae are so high up that youâ€™re either fully paralyzed or youâ€™d be dead very quickly, between seconds and minutes. Snapping the spinal cord will sever the connection between the brain and body, thus, both start to die.

No way anyone will read this but with the whole breathing in and tensing when being tied up thing it's generally more helpful to bear down on your diaphragm like you're straining on the toilet but without the lower abdominal muscles (if you struggle to do this taking a big breath and then exhaling while holding the tension can help) and tense up so that you can still actively breathe because 1) it's super apparent if you're holding your breath and it's easy to force someone to exhale by hitting them and 2) holding your breath is super unsustainable and it's easy to just end up exhaling. Your breathing will be more shallow while you're bearing down on your diaphragm but it'll expand your chest sufficiently and will typically change your posture enough to make you larger. I've tested this method sufficiently to know that it'll work well enough to escape in an emergency.  Quick edit: Also if you're ever holding your breath for some reason not to puff out your cheeks, you want that air to be in your lungs so your lungs can get as much oxygen out of that air as possible. Even if you puff them out when you start to feel uncomfortable there's still some oxygen in that air and it can be useful to help you sustain a breath hold

Is that a real criminal?
I have taken karate and Tae Kwon Do classes for a little more than 6 years. If you're in a chokehold like the one at 9:18, you should NOT immediately try to snap your kidnapper's neck. It's dangerous and inefficient because you waste valuable time, effort, and energy trying to reach backwards in an awkward position. Instead, you should twist your head towards the crook of your attacker's arm to get some breathing room. You want to do this fast before they can clamp down their arm tight around your neck. Try to elbow them in the diaphragm, it's located right in the middle of their chest below their ribs. If you can't, it's fine, you just want to disable/hurt them enough that they loosen their grip. As you elbow them, stomp out with your opposite foot. This sets up your stance to throw them: with the other arm than the one you elbowed them with, grab their forearm. Then with the other arm, grab their tricep, or the bit of sleeve under their tricep. You want to move both your arms at the same time, in unison, as you throw your attacker. Make sure that you twist your hips in line with your throw. This will move your back leg (the one that hasn't stepped out) into a position that is more comfortable and gives power to the throw. While you throw them, you want to make sure that you're throwing them almost straight up and down, as opposed to over and around. This gives power to the throw and ensures that they're incapacitated while you run as fast as you can out of there.

Most modern matches are safety matches, which means they're designed to only be able to be lighted on the strips on the side of the box. The logic behind the tape one is that duct table rips easily horizontally so by doing that the tape would break.
The breathing hack might actually work if done correctly, your goal is basically to make yourself as big as you can. Same for when they tie your wrists, instead of holding the inner sides of your wrists together, you only touch with the top inner sides (in order to hide that you're separating the rest of the wrist). Also if the kidnapper is dumb enough, you can put your wrists side by side (only sides touching).  Another actual tip, if you are zip tied you can break them by doing the same thing you did to break the duct tape, the only other step is to tighten the zip ties first, as this creates more tension. You can also loop something (seatbelt, belt, shoelace, ect) through the zip tie and step on it to create the force needed (which is helpful for people who aren't strong enough to snap zip ties as is).

seeing that the kidnapped person gifts the kidnappers a tv or a playstation is very unlikely though there is a phenomenon known as the stockholm syndrome(from Wikipedia: Stockholm syndrome is a condition in which hostages develop a psychological bond with their captors during captivity.). It is very unlikely. The most popular example and the derivative of its name was in Stockholm on the 23rd to 28th of august 1973. A man tried to rob one of the largest banks in sweden with his friend; and failed. So they took 4 employees as hostages and kept them for 6 days in one of the bank's vault. When the hostages were released, none of them would testify against neither of their captors tl;dr: gifting your captor something expensive is very unlikely. But begging for mercy or not testifying against them has a very low chance but might happen
So basically Stockholm syndrome but in the form of a skit.

A square know for anyone uninitiated is basically when you do a normal knot but do right over left then left over right or vice versa (yes, itâ€™s so easy that Iâ€™d bet many readers already do it naturally). It just makes the knot a square shaped where each side is supporting the other instead of creating a normal loop and a sideways loop, which is more likely to fall out. A square knot is also easier to untie if you know how to untie it. If you tie knots even somewhat regularly, youâ€™ll probably want to learn a square knot since itâ€™s so easy yet effective. In fact, if you do something similar to a square knot with your shoe strings, you end up with a knot that doesnâ€™t come undone accidentally (a single square knot is less likely to come undone than a double non-square knot). If you want to know more about the shoe tying thing, look up Going Deep with David Reece shoe tying method and it hopefully will pop up.

Yeah, the match thing will only work with a specific type of match that isn't very common. See, matches require two substances + friction to light. For safety, only ONE of the substances is put on the actual match - the other is on the scraping surface on the matchbox. This is much safer as matches can't accidentally light in the box, so it's very rare to see ones you can strike on, say, a dungeon wall (at least afaik, i havent exactly looked for them but every match i've seen has been the safer kind)

Reality in Chenzhou There is a saying in modern China, â€œIn the old days, bandits were deep in the mountain; nowadays, they are in police uniforms.â€ Police are supposed to serve the people, but they have become the CCP's weapons to attack innocent people in its persecution of Falun Gong. In Chenzhou City, which Xi visited, many Falun Gong practitioners have been targeted for their faith. Below are a few examples.  Mafia-Style Robbery  Mr. Li Muduo, former employee of the Suxian Industrial and Commercial Bank, had poor health since childhood. After he began to practice Falun Gong, not only did he recover from his numerous illnesses but he also became a better citizen following the principles of Truthfulness-Compassion-Forbearance. During a major flood in 1998, he donated 3,000 yuan and was praised by officials. When wildfires broke out in a nearby mountain, he volunteered to rescue stranded people.  After the persecution of Falun Gong began in July 1999, however, Mr. Li was detained for three months in 2000, and his home was ransacked twice. The police seized his cash and bank deposit book and took pictures of him and his wife. With forged IDs, the police then took money from the couple's bank accounts.  When Mr. Li went to Beijing again in 2001 to appeal for justice for Falun Gong, officials took him to a labor camp for a one-year term. His employer later fired him, leaving his family in poverty.  Ms. Fan Liying, a kindergarten teacher in the Beihu District, learned to be a better person by following the Falun Gong teachings and treated children with kindness. Because of her belief, she was detained ten times and demoted from her position. The former teacher became a babysitter and later a cleaner. Between pay cuts and police-imposed fines, she lost 110,000 yuan (or $16,000) in total.  Wife Imprisoned for Seeking Justice for Husbandâ€™s Death  Ms. Li Jumei, a 63-year-old elementary school teacher in Jiahe Country of Chenzhou, used to suffer from bone cancer. With no money for medical treatment, she attempted suicide multiple times due to the pain: she threw herself onto a railroad track, jumped into a river, and swallowed a large number of sleeping pills. Fortunately, she was rescued all three times.  Three months after beginning to practice Falun Gong, Ms. Li became totally healthy. Health professionals were amazed and asked her for a copy of Zhuan Falun, the main book of Falun Gong. Ms. Liâ€™s husband, Mr. Guo Huisheng, who worked at the Jiahe Legal Office, became interested and also took up Falun Gong. All the time you were doing the match thing, before you struck the match, I  was thinking that I bet you bought the wrong kind of matches, and you did. There are matches that require something like the strip on the side of the box to light, often called safety matches, or strike on box matches and there are matches that just require a rough surface like rock (or concrete blocks) to work and you'll often see them for sale with camping or outdoor equipment, called strike anywhere.  They probably used strike anywhere matches, they come in green now which those were and she had a short strike.  You can light strike on box matches without the strip, which causes a chemical reaction to happen, but you need to strike it a long distance and the right surface.

I don't know if someone already said this but arrivederci is indeed one way to say "bye" in Italian. It is used in a formal context and/or said to people you don't really know personally but pay your respects to as you're leaving, such as, for example, a school professor or a store owner. The word comes from putting the words "a rivederci" together, which basically translates to "to seeing each other again".

Just in case anyone's wondering: Snapping someone's neck (at least the way it's shown in movies and in this video) is total fiction. The human neck isn't a twig, it requires a great deal of force to break, the kind of force most people won't be able to generate, especially in one swift, smooth motion. If it really was that easy, we'd be seeing a lot more broken necks from people getting punched in boxing. So that duct tape thing worked because duct tape is designed to rip when force is applied from two different directions (in this case, out and at a diagonal). It works regardless of the number of layers of duct tape because each layer will rip individually with the force. It also works on zip ties but you have to apply physical pressure from another source -- so you can break out if you slam the zip ties against your thigh while also pulling out and at a diagonal (though it does hurt).

2021 Oct 10
Cursory glance at the comments suggests that nobody has answered this yet, so let me be the first. No, you can't just reach back and snap someone's neck from a disadvantaged position. The body mechanics are all wrong. You wouldn't know it watching tv and movies, where people go around snapping necks like it's nothing, but it isn't really that simple. There would be far fewer people out there doing judo, jujitsu, wrestling, or playing American football if the human neck were that fragile.

D-Does Danny not know about strike-anywhere matches? Cause those were definitely strike-on-box...   You wouldn't be able to light those off the wall cause there's no phosphorus on the matchhead, only sulfur. The little strip on the box is phosphorus which lights the match when it hits the sulfur with enough friction. Strike-anywhere matches have both sulfur and phosphorus in the head so you just need friction.  Danny had strike-on-box matches, he wouldn't have been able to light them off the wall at all, that's why he was struggling with it during the zip tie hack.

Most matches you'll find in everyday life are "safety matches".  They can only be lit when struck against a specially prepared friction surface.  The material on the match head has to be combined with chemicals in the striking surface to cause the chemical reaction leading to the fire.  There are "non-safety" matches (aka "strike anywhere matches") that can be lit on any kind of dry surface with enough friction, but they tend to be just a bit more dangerous because they can in principle inadvertently be lit when they rub against things like the side of their box or other matches.
As Bruno Bucciarati once famously said, â€œArrivederci, losers.â€
